وهو أيضا يتفرع: اس مذکورہ بالا مسئلہ کی ایک دوسری اختلافی اصل پر تفریح ذکر کی گئی ہے اور وہ یہ ہے اگر کسی وجہ سے نماز کا وصف مثلا فرضیت وغیرہ باطل ہو جائے تو اصل نماز باطل ہوگی یا نہیں [یحین؟] کے نزدیک اصل صلاح باطل نہ ہوگی بلکہ محض وصف باطل ہوتا ہے اور وصف کے بطلان سے اصل کا بطلان لازم نہیں آتا جبکہ امام محمد کے نزدیک وصف کے بطلان سے اصل بھی باطل ہو جاتی ہے جیسے اوپر والے مسئلہ میں جمعہ کے بعد جو چار رکعت نماز پڑھی اصل جمعہ کے صحیح ہونے کی وجہ سے ان کی فرضیت باطل ہوگئی کیونکہ اس کے ذمہ ظہر کی نماز بھی نہیں تھی لیکن اب فل ہوئی یا نہیں شیخین کے مذہب کے اعتبار سے نقل ہوگئی کیونکہ وصف کے بطلان سے اصل نماز باطل نہیں ہوتی، لیکن امام محمد کے نزدیک نفل بھی نہ ہوئی کیونکہ ان کے نزدیک وصف کا بطلان اصل کے بطلان کو ستلزم ہے لیکن یہ [یکم؟] اس صورت میں ہے جب کہ اس نماز سے نمازی اپنے ذمہ سے بری نہیں ہوسکتا، اور اگر اس نماز سے نمازی زمہ کے بری ہو سکتا ہے تو اس صورت میں وصف کا بطلان اصل کے بطلان کو جملہ عبادات میں امام محمد کے نزدیک بھی مستلزم نہیں ہے۔ دیکھئے اگر کسی نے اپنی طرف سے صحیح ہونے کی حالت میں حج بدل کرایا یا مریض تھا اور پھر [سیح؟] ہو گیا تو ان دونوں صورتوں میں وصف یعنی فرضیت حج باطل ہو گئی لیکن اصل حج یعنی نفلی امر کی طرف سے ادا ہو جائے گا۔
And it also branches: This mentioned issue has a second difference of principle on which a furua is mentioned. It is: If for some reason the attribute of prayer, e.g. fardiyyah, becomes invalid, does the original prayer become invalid or not? According to the [Shaykhayn?] the original prayer does not become invalid; rather only the attribute becomes invalid, and the invalidation of the attribute does not necessitate the invalidation of the original. While according to Imam Muhammad, the invalidation of the attribute also causes the original to become invalid. For example, in the previous issue, the four rak'ahs prayed after Jumu'ah: due to the validity of Jumu'ah, their fardiyyah became invalid because there was no Zhuhr prayer owed on him. But did they become nafl or not? According to the madhhab of the Shaykhayn, they became nafl because the invalidation of the attribute does not invalidate the original prayer. But according to Imam Muhammad, they did not become nafl because according to him the invalidation of the attribute entails the invalidation of the original. But this is only in the case when the worshipper cannot discharge his obligation through this prayer. And if the worshipper can discharge his obligation through this prayer, then in that case the invalidation of the attribute does not entail the invalidation of the original, in all acts of worship, even according to Imam Muhammad. For example, if someone hired a Hajj badal while he was himself in a state of being able to perform Hajj, or he was sick and then recovered, then in both cases the attribute i.e. fardiyyah of Hajj became invalid, but the original Hajj will be performed on behalf of nafl.
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage is presenting a furua (application) of an earlier discussed usul principle: the effect of the invalidation of a legal attribute on the original act. The text states the positions of the Shaykhayn (Abu Hanifa and Abu Yusuf) and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani. The rule: for the Shaykhayn, if an attribute like fardiyyah becomes invalid (e.g., because the obligation was already fulfilled), the original act (asl) remains valid; for Imam Muhammad, the asl also becomes invalid. The text then provides an example: after Jumu'ah, if one prays four rak'ahs thinking it is Zhuhr, but Jumu'ah was valid, those rak'ahs become nafl according to the Shaykhayn, but according to Imam Muhammad they are invalid. However, an exception is noted: if the worshipper can discharge an obligation through the act (e.g., hiring a Hajj badal when he is healthy, or recovering from illness), then even Imam Muhammad agrees that the asl remains valid (as nafl). This is a nuanced rule with an istithna' (exception).

Key Terms
وصف (wasf): Legal attribute (e.g., fardiyyah, obligation) of an act of worship.
اصل (asl): The original act itself, as opposed to its attribute.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Shaykhayn, if a person prays four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah thinking it is Zhuhr, but Jumu'ah was valid, what happens to those four rak'ahs?
A) They are invalid and must be repeated.
B) They become nafl.
C) They are counted as missed fard.
D) They are valid as Zhuhr.

Key Takeaway
The invalidation of a legal attribute (wasf) does not necessarily invalidate the original act (asl); the Hanafi school's mufta bihi position, following the Shaykhayn, maintains the act's validity, often as nafl, with an exception for cases where the obligation cannot be discharged.

Absolute Intention for Nafl and Masnun Fasts
Stating that for nafl and masnun fasts, absolute intention suffices without specifying the type

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi rule that absolute intention suffices for nafl and masnun fasts, identify the time limit for intention, and apply it to a scenario.

Core Idea
Absolute intention suffices for nafl and masnun fasts; specification is not required until midday.

This lesson examines a key ruling from the Hanafi school regarding intention for voluntary and recommended fasts. Unlike obligatory prayers, which require specification, fasting has been granted a special dispensation. Understanding this rule is essential for issuing correct fatwas on fasting.

Guided Path
1
Identify the fast types covered
The ruling applies to nafl (voluntary) and masnun (recommended) fasts, not fard or wajib fasts.
Masnun fasts include Mondays, Thursdays, etc.
2
State the ruling on intention
Absolute intention (niyyah mutlaqah) suffices; specification (ta'yin) is not required. The fast can also be performed with the intention of another obligatory fast (e.g., qada).
This is a dispensation unique to fasting.
3
Note the time limit for intention
For nafl fasts, the intention can be made before zawal (midday) but not after. For masnun fasts, the same rule applies.
This is based on Sharh Wiqayah.
4
Compare with supererogatory prayers
Supererogatory prayers (salat) require ta'yin (specification), but fasting does not. This highlights the taysir in fasting.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وينبغي ان تلحق الصيامات : اگر کوئی شخص نفل یا مسنون روزے رکھے تو اس کے لئے مطلق نیت کافی ہے اس میں صلوات مسنونہ کی طرح تعیین کی ضرورت نہیں ہے۔ وهذا الضرب من الصوم ينادى بمطلق النية و بنية النفل و بنية واجب آخر ( تار تار خانی ج ۲ : ۳۵۷) والنفل بنية و بنيته مطلقة قبل الزوال لا بعده (شرح وقایه ج ۱، ص ۲۴۴)
And it is appropriate to attach fasts [to this ruling]: If a person keeps a nafl or masnun fast, then for him an absolute intention is sufficient; in this, specification is not required like in supererogatory prayers. And this type of fast is performed with absolute intention, and with intention of nafl, and with intention of another obligatory [fast]. (Tar Tar Khani vol. 2, p. 357) And the nafl [fast] with intention, and its absolute intention, before zawal, not after. (Sharh Wiqayah vol. 1, p. 244)
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage states a legal rule concerning nafl and masnun fasts: unlike supererogatory prayers which require specification of the prayer (ta'yin), fasting with an absolute intention (mutlaq niyyah) suffices. The text also notes that this type of fast can be performed with an absolute intention, or with the intention of nafl, or even with the intention of another obligatory fast (i.e., if one intends a missed Ramadan fast, it counts for that). Additionally, for nafl fasts, the intention can be made up until midday (zawal), not after. This is a dispensation (taysir) in the Hanafi school.

Key Terms
نیت مطلقة (niyyah mutlaqah): Absolute intention without specifying the type of fast.
صوم مسنون (sawm masnun): Recommended fast (e.g., Mondays, Thursdays, etc.)

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
For a nafl fast, until when can the intention be made?
A) Before dawn (fajr)
B) Before zawal (midday)
C) After zawal
D) At any time during the day

Key Takeaway
For nafl and masnun fasts, absolute intention made before zawal is sufficient.

The Regular Emphasized Sunnah Prayers (Sunan Rawatib): Definition and List
Definition and enumeration of sunan rawatib.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the definition and list of the twelve sunan rawatib and apply the qawida that classifies them as sunan mu'akkadah.

Core Idea
The sunan rawatib are twelve daily rak'ahs that are emphasized (mu'akkadah) and form a regular supererogatory practice.

This lesson introduces the Sunan Rawatib, the regular supererogatory prayers that are emphasized in the Hanafi school. Understanding their definition and count is essential for a mufti to answer common questions about recommended prayers. The passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir lists them and discusses their significance.

Guided Path
1
Identify the definition
From the text, sunan rawatib are the emphasized sunnah prayers that are regular (rawatib) in the day and night.
The term 'rawatib' implies regularity.
2
Count the twelve rak'ahs
List them: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. Total 12.
These are the basic sunan rawatib.
3
Recognize synonym
Note that they are also called sunan mu'akkadah (emphasized sunnahs).
Emphasis means they are strongly recommended, not obligatory.
4
Acknowledge extensions
The text then mentions additional sunnah prayers for Jumu'ah, Tarawih, etc., which are not part of the basic 12 but are also emphasized.
These extensions are considered separate sunan.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
السُّنُ الرَّوَاتِبُ فِي الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ لِيْنَا عَشَرَةَ رَكْعَةً : رَكْعَتَانِ قَبْلَ الْفَجْرِ، وَارْبَعٌ قَبْلَ الظُّهْرِ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَهَا ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَ الْمَغْرِبِ، وَرَكْعَتَانَ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ ، وَفِي صَلَاةِ الْجُمُعَةِ أَرْبَعَ قَبْلَهَا وَأَرْبَعَ بَعْدَهَا، وَالتَّرَاوِيْحُ عِشْرُونَ رَكْعَةً بِعَشْرِ تَسْلِيْمَاتٍ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ فِي لَيَالِي رَمَضَانَ، وَصَلَا الْوِتْرِ عَلَى قَوْلِهِمَا، وَصَلَاةُ الْعِيْدَيْنِ فِي إِحْدَى الرِّوَايَتَيْنِ، وَصَلَاةُ الْكُسُوْفِ عَلَى الصَّحِيحِ ، وَقِيلَ : وَاجِبَةٌ، وَصَلَاةُ الْخُسُوْفِ وَالْإِسْتِسْقَاءِ عَلَى قَوْلٍ. 

ترجمه سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار و ر کھتیں ہیں دورکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دورکعت نظیر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر اور عیدین کی نماز دور وانیوں میں سے ایک میں اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے اور نماز خوف اور استقاء ایک قول پر ۔ 

تشریح : اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے سفن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ موکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن موکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے ، دورکعت ظہر کے بعد ، اور دورکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگر چہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی یہ ہے۔ 

(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص : ٦٣٦) 

وفي صلاة الجمعة : جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات ہیں ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے اگر کسی نے چار چار کعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع ، ج) بس : ۶۴۴) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگر چہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور دتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تر اویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔ صلاة الوتر : صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لیکر وتر کی سنیت کی
The sunan al-rawatib in the day and night are twelve rak'ahs: two rakahs before Fajr, four before Zhuhr, two after it, two after Maghrib, two after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four before it and four after it. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to their saying, and the two Eid prayers in one of the two narrations, and the eclipse prayer according to the correct view, and it is said it is obligatory. And the lunar eclipse and istisqa prayers according to a saying.

Translation: The Sunan Mu'akkadah in the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, and four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, and two rak'ahs after it, and two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the saying of the two [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], and Eid prayer in one of the two narrations, and according to the correct saying, eclipse prayer, and it is said it is obligatory, and prayers of lunar eclipse and istisqa' according to a saying.

Commentary: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the Sunan Mu'akkadah. Sunan Rawatib are those sunnahs that are mu'akkadah; therefore they are also called Sunan Mu'akkadah. The Sunan Rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, two after Zhuhr, two after Maghrib, and two after Isha. But among these, the two before Fajr are close to being obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement. For this reason, some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnahs, although this opinion of obligation is not the mufta bihi (relied upon). (Bada'i al-Sana'i' vol. 1, p. 636)

And regarding Jumu'ah prayer: In Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah are sunnah mu'akkadah, and four after Jumu'ah. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and this is narrated from 'Ali. And the best is to pray four and then two to exit the disagreement.' 

And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams; that is the saying of the majority of scholars. If someone prayed four rak'ahs and performed the first sitting, that is also correct. And its number is twenty rak'ahs with ten taslimahs in five tarwihahs, each two taslimahs is a tarwihah, and this is the saying of the general scholars. (Bada'i' vol... p. 644) After Isha: Some scholars say that the time of Tarawih is after Isha and before Witr. Some say the entire night is time for Tarawih. The majority opinion is that after Isha the time for Tarawih begins, whether one prays before Witr or after, although the best is after Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; it is explicitly stated in Zahiriyyah etc. For this reason it is said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada after the time passes. Some scholars say that qada can be prayed as long as Ramadan does not pass, and some say it can be prayed until the next night arrives. 

Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; the Sahibayn took this narration for the sunniyyah of Witr...
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir enumerates the Sunan Rawatib (regular supererogatory prayers) that are emphasized (mu'akkadah). The basic list includes 12 rak'ahs: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. The matn then extends to Jumu'ah (4 before, 4 after), Tarawih (20 rak'ahs), Witr (according to the Sahibayn), Eid, eclipse, and istisqa. The commentary adds: - The Fajr sunnah is so emphasized that some scholars considered it obligatory, but the mufta bihi is that it is sunnah. - Regarding Jumu'ah, Imam Abu Yusuf holds that the after-sunnah is six rak'ahs (4+2) to reconcile conflicting hadith; the preferred practice is to pray 4 then 2. - Tarawih is 20 rak'ahs in 10 salams; the time is after Isha; if missed, some say no qada, others allow qada within Ramadan or until the next night. - Witr: Sahibayn say it is sunnah; Imam Abu Hanifa has multiple reports, the relied upon being that it is wajib? Actually the text says 'sunniyyah', but the discussion here says 'sunnah' according to Sahibayn, and one narration from Abu Hanifa also says sunnah. This reflects internal Hanafi difference.

Key Terms
سنن رواتب (sunan rawatib): Regular supererogatory prayers that are emphasized (mu'akkadah).
سنن مؤكدة (sunan mu'akkadah): Emphasized sunnah prayers.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
How many rak'ahs are in the Sunan Rawatib per day?
A) 10
B) 12
C) 14
D) 20

Key Takeaway
The Sunan Rawatib are twelve emphasized sunnah rak'ahs daily; their regular performance is strongly recommended.

Furuat al-Qawaid — Derived Applications
intermediate
5 min
Fajr Sunnah: High Emphasis but Still Sunnah
Discussion of the Fajr sunnah's emphasis.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the ruling of the Fajr sunnah, identify its high emphasis, and state the mufta bihi position.

Core Idea
The Fajr sunnah is the most emphasized sunnah, but the mufta bihi is that it is not wajib.

Among the sunan rawatib, the two rak'ahs before Fajr hold a special status. The text notes they are 'close to wajib' due to the strong emphasis. However, the relied-upon position remains sunnah. This lesson explores that nuance.

Guided Path
1
Locate the Fajr sunnah in the list
It is the first item: two rak'ahs before Fajr.
2
Understand the phrase 'close to wajib'
The commentary explains that due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement, some scholars considered it obligatory.
This is not the mufta bihi.
3
Identify the mufta bihi
The text explicitly says that the opinion of obligation is not mufta bihi; the school's position is sunnah mu'akkadah.
Refer to the fatwa hierarchy.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
السُّنُ الرَّوَاتِبُ فِي الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ لِيْنَا عَشَرَةَ رَكْعَةً : رَكْعَتَانِ قَبْلَ الْفَجْرِ، وَارْبَعٌ قَبْلَ الظُّهْرِ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَهَا ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَ الْمَغْرِبِ، وَرَكْعَتَانَ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ ، وَفِي صَلَاةِ الْجُمُعَةِ أَرْبَعَ قَبْلَهَا وَأَرْبَعَ بَعْدَهَا، وَالتَّرَاوِيْحُ عِشْرُونَ رَكْعَةً بِعَشْرِ تَسْلِيْمَاتٍ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ فِي لَيَالِي رَمَضَانَ، وَصَلَا الْوِتْرِ عَلَى قَوْلِهِمَا، وَصَلَاةُ الْعِيْدَيْنِ فِي إِحْدَى الرِّوَايَتَيْنِ، وَصَلَاةُ الْكُسُوْفِ عَلَى الصَّحِيحِ ، وَقِيلَ : وَاجِبَةٌ، وَصَلَاةُ الْخُسُوْفِ وَالْإِسْتِسْقَاءِ عَلَى قَوْلٍ. 

ترجمه سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار و ر کھتیں ہیں دورکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دورکعت نظیر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر اور عیدین کی نماز دور وانیوں میں سے ایک میں اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے اور نماز خوف اور استقاء ایک قول پر ۔ 

تشریح : اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے سفن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ موکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن موکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے ، دورکعت ظہر کے بعد ، اور دورکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگر چہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی یہ ہے۔ 

(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص : ٦٣٦) 

وفي صلاة الجمعة : جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات ہیں ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے اگر کسی نے چار چار کعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع ، ج) بس : ۶۴۴) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگر چہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور دتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تر اویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔ صلاة الوتر : صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لیکر وتر کی سنیت کی
The sunan al-rawatib in the day and night are twelve rak'ahs: two rakahs before Fajr, four before Zhuhr, two after it, two after Maghrib, two after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four before it and four after it. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to their saying, and the two Eid prayers in one of the two narrations, and the eclipse prayer according to the correct view, and it is said it is obligatory. And the lunar eclipse and istisqa prayers according to a saying.

Translation: The Sunan Mu'akkadah in the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, and four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, and two rak'ahs after it, and two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the saying of the two [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], and Eid prayer in one of the two narrations, and according to the correct saying, eclipse prayer, and it is said it is obligatory, and prayers of lunar eclipse and istisqa' according to a saying.

Commentary: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the Sunan Mu'akkadah. Sunan Rawatib are those sunnahs that are mu'akkadah; therefore they are also called Sunan Mu'akkadah. The Sunan Rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, two after Zhuhr, two after Maghrib, and two after Isha. But among these, the two before Fajr are close to being obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement. For this reason, some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnahs, although this opinion of obligation is not the mufta bihi (relied upon). (Bada'i al-Sana'i' vol. 1, p. 636)

And regarding Jumu'ah prayer: In Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah are sunnah mu'akkadah, and four after Jumu'ah. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and this is narrated from 'Ali. And the best is to pray four and then two to exit the disagreement.' 

And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams; that is the saying of the majority of scholars. If someone prayed four rak'ahs and performed the first sitting, that is also correct. And its number is twenty rak'ahs with ten taslimahs in five tarwihahs, each two taslimahs is a tarwihah, and this is the saying of the general scholars. (Bada'i' vol... p. 644) After Isha: Some scholars say that the time of Tarawih is after Isha and before Witr. Some say the entire night is time for Tarawih. The majority opinion is that after Isha the time for Tarawih begins, whether one prays before Witr or after, although the best is after Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; it is explicitly stated in Zahiriyyah etc. For this reason it is said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada after the time passes. Some scholars say that qada can be prayed as long as Ramadan does not pass, and some say it can be prayed until the next night arrives. 

Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; the Sahibayn took this narration for the sunniyyah of Witr...
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir enumerates the Sunan Rawatib (regular supererogatory prayers) that are emphasized (mu'akkadah). The basic list includes 12 rak'ahs: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. The matn then extends to Jumu'ah (4 before, 4 after), Tarawih (20 rak'ahs), Witr (according to the Sahibayn), Eid, eclipse, and istisqa. The commentary adds: - The Fajr sunnah is so emphasized that some scholars considered it obligatory, but the mufta bihi is that it is sunnah. - Regarding Jumu'ah, Imam Abu Yusuf holds that the after-sunnah is six rak'ahs (4+2) to reconcile conflicting hadith; the preferred practice is to pray 4 then 2. - Tarawih is 20 rak'ahs in 10 salams; the time is after Isha; if missed, some say no qada, others allow qada within Ramadan or until the next night. - Witr: Sahibayn say it is sunnah; Imam Abu Hanifa has multiple reports, the relied upon being that it is wajib? Actually the text says 'sunniyyah', but the discussion here says 'sunnah' according to Sahibayn, and one narration from Abu Hanifa also says sunnah. This reflects internal Hanafi difference.

Key Terms
قريب واجبات (qarib wājibāt): Close to obligations; a description of the Fajr sunnah's emphasis.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the mufta bihi ruling of the Fajr sunnah in the Hanafi school?
A) Wajib
B) Sunnah mu'akkadah
C) Fard
D) Mubah

Key Takeaway
The Fajr sunnah is highly emphasized but remains sunnah mu'akkadah, not wajib.

Furuat al-Qawaid — Derived Applications
intermediate
5 min
Jumu'ah Sunnah: Four Before and Four (or Six) After
Detailing the sunnah for Jumu'ah prayer.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the sunnah rak'ahs for Jumu'ah and identify the ikhtilaf regarding the after-prayer.

Core Idea
Before Jumu'ah, four rak'ahs are sunnah; after, four are sunnah, but Abu Yusuf says six.

The Jumu'ah prayer has additional sunnah prayers. The text mentions four before and four after. However, Imam Abu Yusuf adds two more after, making six. This lesson explores that intra-Hanafi difference.

Guided Path
1
Identify the list for Jumu'ah
The text says: four before Jumu'ah and four after.
2
Note Abu Yusuf's view
The commentary adds that according to Abu Yusuf, there are six after Jumu'ah (four plus two).
This is based on a narration from Ali.
3
Resolve the ikhtilaf
The recommended practice is to pray four then two to exit the disagreement.
The mufta bihi is often the four after, but the precautionary approach is accepted.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
السُّنُ الرَّوَاتِبُ فِي الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ لِيْنَا عَشَرَةَ رَكْعَةً : رَكْعَتَانِ قَبْلَ الْفَجْرِ، وَارْبَعٌ قَبْلَ الظُّهْرِ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَهَا ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَ الْمَغْرِبِ، وَرَكْعَتَانَ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ ، وَفِي صَلَاةِ الْجُمُعَةِ أَرْبَعَ قَبْلَهَا وَأَرْبَعَ بَعْدَهَا، وَالتَّرَاوِيْحُ عِشْرُونَ رَكْعَةً بِعَشْرِ تَسْلِيْمَاتٍ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ فِي لَيَالِي رَمَضَانَ، وَصَلَا الْوِتْرِ عَلَى قَوْلِهِمَا، وَصَلَاةُ الْعِيْدَيْنِ فِي إِحْدَى الرِّوَايَتَيْنِ، وَصَلَاةُ الْكُسُوْفِ عَلَى الصَّحِيحِ ، وَقِيلَ : وَاجِبَةٌ، وَصَلَاةُ الْخُسُوْفِ وَالْإِسْتِسْقَاءِ عَلَى قَوْلٍ. 

ترجمه سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار و ر کھتیں ہیں دورکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دورکعت نظیر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر اور عیدین کی نماز دور وانیوں میں سے ایک میں اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے اور نماز خوف اور استقاء ایک قول پر ۔ 

تشریح : اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے سفن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ موکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن موکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے ، دورکعت ظہر کے بعد ، اور دورکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگر چہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی یہ ہے۔ 

(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص : ٦٣٦) 

وفي صلاة الجمعة : جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات ہیں ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے اگر کسی نے چار چار کعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع ، ج) بس : ۶۴۴) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگر چہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور دتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تر اویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔ صلاة الوتر : صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لیکر وتر کی سنیت کی
The sunan al-rawatib in the day and night are twelve rak'ahs: two rakahs before Fajr, four before Zhuhr, two after it, two after Maghrib, two after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four before it and four after it. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to their saying, and the two Eid prayers in one of the two narrations, and the eclipse prayer according to the correct view, and it is said it is obligatory. And the lunar eclipse and istisqa prayers according to a saying.

Translation: The Sunan Mu'akkadah in the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, and four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, and two rak'ahs after it, and two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the saying of the two [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], and Eid prayer in one of the two narrations, and according to the correct saying, eclipse prayer, and it is said it is obligatory, and prayers of lunar eclipse and istisqa' according to a saying.

Commentary: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the Sunan Mu'akkadah. Sunan Rawatib are those sunnahs that are mu'akkadah; therefore they are also called Sunan Mu'akkadah. The Sunan Rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, two after Zhuhr, two after Maghrib, and two after Isha. But among these, the two before Fajr are close to being obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement. For this reason, some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnahs, although this opinion of obligation is not the mufta bihi (relied upon). (Bada'i al-Sana'i' vol. 1, p. 636)

And regarding Jumu'ah prayer: In Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah are sunnah mu'akkadah, and four after Jumu'ah. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and this is narrated from 'Ali. And the best is to pray four and then two to exit the disagreement.' 

And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams; that is the saying of the majority of scholars. If someone prayed four rak'ahs and performed the first sitting, that is also correct. And its number is twenty rak'ahs with ten taslimahs in five tarwihahs, each two taslimahs is a tarwihah, and this is the saying of the general scholars. (Bada'i' vol... p. 644) After Isha: Some scholars say that the time of Tarawih is after Isha and before Witr. Some say the entire night is time for Tarawih. The majority opinion is that after Isha the time for Tarawih begins, whether one prays before Witr or after, although the best is after Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; it is explicitly stated in Zahiriyyah etc. For this reason it is said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada after the time passes. Some scholars say that qada can be prayed as long as Ramadan does not pass, and some say it can be prayed until the next night arrives. 

Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; the Sahibayn took this narration for the sunniyyah of Witr...
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir enumerates the Sunan Rawatib (regular supererogatory prayers) that are emphasized (mu'akkadah). The basic list includes 12 rak'ahs: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. The matn then extends to Jumu'ah (4 before, 4 after), Tarawih (20 rak'ahs), Witr (according to the Sahibayn), Eid, eclipse, and istisqa. The commentary adds: - The Fajr sunnah is so emphasized that some scholars considered it obligatory, but the mufta bihi is that it is sunnah. - Regarding Jumu'ah, Imam Abu Yusuf holds that the after-sunnah is six rak'ahs (4+2) to reconcile conflicting hadith; the preferred practice is to pray 4 then 2. - Tarawih is 20 rak'ahs in 10 salams; the time is after Isha; if missed, some say no qada, others allow qada within Ramadan or until the next night. - Witr: Sahibayn say it is sunnah; Imam Abu Hanifa has multiple reports, the relied upon being that it is wajib? Actually the text says 'sunniyyah', but the discussion here says 'sunnah' according to Sahibayn, and one narration from Abu Hanifa also says sunnah. This reflects internal Hanafi difference.

Key Terms
سنة الجمعة (sunnat al-jumu'ah): The sunnah prayers associated with Jumu'ah prayer.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
How many sunnah rak'ahs are prayed after Jumu'ah according to the majority Hanafi view?
A) Two
B) Four
C) Six
D) Eight

Key Takeaway
The sunnah after Jumu'ah is four rak'ahs according to the mufta bihi, but a precautionary addition of two is allowed.

Tarawih: Twenty Rak'ahs of Night Prayer in Ramadan
Details on Tarawih prayer number, time, ruling, and qada dispute.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the number, time, and ruling of Tarawih, and explain the dispute on qada.

Core Idea
Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs, sunnah mu'akkadah, prayed after Isha; if missed, qada is not required after the month.

Tarawih is a special sunnah of Ramadan. The text specifies its number and mentions disagreements on its time and qada. This lesson covers these details for a mufti's use.

Guided Path
1
State the number of rak'ahs
Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams.
Some say four rak'ahs at a time is also allowed.
2
Identify the time
After Isha prayer, before or after Witr. The best is after Isha and before Witr.
Some say the entire night is time.
3
Classify the ruling
Tarawih is sunnah mu'akkadah.
It is not wajib.
4
Understand the qada dispute
According to the majority, there is no qada after Ramadan. Some allow qada until Ramadan ends or the next night.
The mufta bihi is that qada is not required after the month.

Source Text

ترجمه سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار و ر کھتیں ہیں دورکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دورکعت نظیر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر اور عیدین کی نماز دور وانیوں میں سے ایک میں اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے اور نماز خوف اور استقاء ایک قول پر ۔ 

تشریح : اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے سفن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ موکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن موکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے ، دورکعت ظہر کے بعد ، اور دورکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگر چہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی یہ ہے۔ 

(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص : ٦٣٦) 

وفي صلاة الجمعة : جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات ہیں ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے اگر کسی نے چار چار کعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع ، ج) بس : ۶۴۴) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگر چہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور دتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تر اویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔ صلاة الوتر : صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لیکر وتر کی سنیت کی
The sunan al-rawatib in the day and night are twelve rak'ahs: two rakahs before Fajr, four before Zhuhr, two after it, two after Maghrib, two after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four before it and four after it. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to their saying, and the two Eid prayers in one of the two narrations, and the eclipse prayer according to the correct view, and it is said it is obligatory. And the lunar eclipse and istisqa prayers according to a saying.

Translation: The Sunan Mu'akkadah in the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, and four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, and two rak'ahs after it, and two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the saying of the two [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], and Eid prayer in one of the two narrations, and according to the correct saying, eclipse prayer, and it is said it is obligatory, and prayers of lunar eclipse and istisqa' according to a saying.

Commentary: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the Sunan Mu'akkadah. Sunan Rawatib are those sunnahs that are mu'akkadah; therefore they are also called Sunan Mu'akkadah. The Sunan Rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, two after Zhuhr, two after Maghrib, and two after Isha. But among these, the two before Fajr are close to being obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement. For this reason, some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnahs, although this opinion of obligation is not the mufta bihi (relied upon). (Bada'i al-Sana'i' vol. 1, p. 636)

And regarding Jumu'ah prayer: In Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah are sunnah mu'akkadah, and four after Jumu'ah. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and this is narrated from 'Ali. And the best is to pray four and then two to exit the disagreement.' 

And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams; that is the saying of the majority of scholars. If someone prayed four rak'ahs and performed the first sitting, that is also correct. And its number is twenty rak'ahs with ten taslimahs in five tarwihahs, each two taslimahs is a tarwihah, and this is the saying of the general scholars. (Bada'i' vol... p. 644) After Isha: Some scholars say that the time of Tarawih is after Isha and before Witr. Some say the entire night is time for Tarawih. The majority opinion is that after Isha the time for Tarawih begins, whether one prays before Witr or after, although the best is after Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; it is explicitly stated in Zahiriyyah etc. For this reason it is said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada after the time passes. Some scholars say that qada can be prayed as long as Ramadan does not pass, and some say it can be prayed until the next night arrives. 

Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; the Sahibayn took this narration for the sunniyyah of Witr...

Commentary
This passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir enumerates the Sunan Rawatib (regular supererogatory prayers) that are emphasized (mu'akkadah). The basic list includes 12 rak'ahs: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. تراويح (tarawih): Night prayers in Ramadan, twenty rak'ahs.

Witr Prayer: Sunnah or Wajib? The Internal Hanafi Dispute
Internal Hanafi dispute on the legal status of Witr.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the Hanafi internal dispute on Witr's ruling and state the mufta bihi.

Core Idea
According to the Sahibayn, Witr is sunnah; according to Abu Hanifa's preferred view, it is wajib.

Witr prayer is a subject of internal Hanafi difference. The text presents the Sahibayn's view that it is sunnah, but the mufta bihi in the school is that it is wajib. This lesson explores that ikhtilaf.

Guided Path
1
Read the text's statement
The text says 'Salat al-Witr 'ala qawlihima' (Witr prayer according to their saying). 'They' refers to Abu Yusuf and Muhammad.
This indicates the Sahibayn's position.
2
Contrast with Abu Hanifa's view
Imam Abu Hanifa has three narrations; the preferred view is that Witr is wajib.
One narration says it is sunnah mu'akkadah.
3
Determine the mufta bihi
The relied-upon position in the Hanafi school is that Witr is wajib.
This is for fatwa purposes.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
السُّنُ الرَّوَاتِبُ فِي الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ لِيْنَا عَشَرَةَ رَكْعَةً : رَكْعَتَانِ قَبْلَ الْفَجْرِ، وَارْبَعٌ قَبْلَ الظُّهْرِ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَهَا ، وَرَكْعَتَانِ بَعْدَ الْمَغْرِبِ، وَرَكْعَتَانَ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ ، وَفِي صَلَاةِ الْجُمُعَةِ أَرْبَعَ قَبْلَهَا وَأَرْبَعَ بَعْدَهَا، وَالتَّرَاوِيْحُ عِشْرُونَ رَكْعَةً بِعَشْرِ تَسْلِيْمَاتٍ بَعْدَ الْعِشَاءِ فِي لَيَالِي رَمَضَانَ، وَصَلَا الْوِتْرِ عَلَى قَوْلِهِمَا، وَصَلَاةُ الْعِيْدَيْنِ فِي إِحْدَى الرِّوَايَتَيْنِ، وَصَلَاةُ الْكُسُوْفِ عَلَى الصَّحِيحِ ، وَقِيلَ : وَاجِبَةٌ، وَصَلَاةُ الْخُسُوْفِ وَالْإِسْتِسْقَاءِ عَلَى قَوْلٍ. 

ترجمه سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار و ر کھتیں ہیں دورکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دورکعت نظیر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر اور عیدین کی نماز دور وانیوں میں سے ایک میں اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے اور نماز خوف اور استقاء ایک قول پر ۔ 

تشریح : اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے سفن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ موکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن موکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے ، دورکعت ظہر کے بعد ، اور دورکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگر چہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی یہ ہے۔ 

(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص : ٦٣٦) 

وفي صلاة الجمعة : جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات ہیں ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے اگر کسی نے چار چار کعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع ، ج) بس : ۶۴۴) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگر چہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور دتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تر اویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔ صلاة الوتر : صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لیکر وتر کی سنیت کی
The sunan al-rawatib in the day and night are twelve rak'ahs: two rakahs before Fajr, four before Zhuhr, two after it, two after Maghrib, two after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four before it and four after it. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to their saying, and the two Eid prayers in one of the two narrations, and the eclipse prayer according to the correct view, and it is said it is obligatory. And the lunar eclipse and istisqa prayers according to a saying.

Translation: The Sunan Mu'akkadah in the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, and four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, and two rak'ahs after it, and two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after Isha. And in Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the saying of the two [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], and Eid prayer in one of the two narrations, and according to the correct saying, eclipse prayer, and it is said it is obligatory, and prayers of lunar eclipse and istisqa' according to a saying.

Commentary: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the Sunan Mu'akkadah. Sunan Rawatib are those sunnahs that are mu'akkadah; therefore they are also called Sunan Mu'akkadah. The Sunan Rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zhuhr, two after Zhuhr, two after Maghrib, and two after Isha. But among these, the two before Fajr are close to being obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and discouragement. For this reason, some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnahs, although this opinion of obligation is not the mufta bihi (relied upon). (Bada'i al-Sana'i' vol. 1, p. 636)

And regarding Jumu'ah prayer: In Jumu'ah prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah are sunnah mu'akkadah, and four after Jumu'ah. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and this is narrated from 'Ali. And the best is to pray four and then two to exit the disagreement.' 

And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams; that is the saying of the majority of scholars. If someone prayed four rak'ahs and performed the first sitting, that is also correct. And its number is twenty rak'ahs with ten taslimahs in five tarwihahs, each two taslimahs is a tarwihah, and this is the saying of the general scholars. (Bada'i' vol... p. 644) After Isha: Some scholars say that the time of Tarawih is after Isha and before Witr. Some say the entire night is time for Tarawih. The majority opinion is that after Isha the time for Tarawih begins, whether one prays before Witr or after, although the best is after Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; it is explicitly stated in Zahiriyyah etc. For this reason it is said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada after the time passes. Some scholars say that qada can be prayed as long as Ramadan does not pass, and some say it can be prayed until the next night arrives. 

Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn [Abu Yusuf and Muhammad], Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah; the Sahibayn took this narration for the sunniyyah of Witr...
Source pages p. 166

Commentary
This passage from al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir enumerates the Sunan Rawatib (regular supererogatory prayers) that are emphasized (mu'akkadah). The basic list includes 12 rak'ahs: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zhuhr, 2 after Zhuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after Isha. The matn then extends to Jumu'ah (4 before, 4 after), Tarawih (20 rak'ahs), Witr (according to the Sahibayn), Eid, eclipse, and istisqa. The commentary adds: - The Fajr sunnah is so emphasized that some scholars considered it obligatory, but the mufta bihi is that it is sunnah. - Regarding Jumu'ah, Imam Abu Yusuf holds that the after-sunnah is six rak'ahs (4+2) to reconcile conflicting hadith; the preferred practice is to pray 4 then 2. - Tarawih is 20 rak'ahs in 10 salams; the time is after Isha; if missed, some say no qada, others allow qada within Ramadan or until the next night. - Witr: Sahibayn say it is sunnah; Imam Abu Hanifa has multiple reports, the relied upon being that it is wajib? Actually the text says 'sunniyyah', but the discussion here says 'sunnah' according to Sahibayn, and one narration from Abu Hanifa also says sunnah. This reflects internal Hanafi difference.

Key Terms
وتر (witr): Odd-numbered prayer after Isha.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the mufta bihi ruling of Witr in the Hanafi school?
A) Sunnah
B) Wajib
C) Fard
D) Mustahabb

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school's relied-upon position is that Witr is wajib, despite the Sahibayn's view that it is sunnah.

Furuat al-Qawaid — Derived Applications

Sunnan Rawatib: The Twelve Emphasized Sunnah Prayers
Lists twelve sunnan rawatib and notes Fajr sunnah's status.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to list the twelve sunnan rawatib and explain why the Fajr sunnah is classified as sunnah mu'akkada, not wajib, according to the Hanafi school's relied-upon position.

Core Idea
The twelve sunnan rawatib are sunnah mu'akkada; the Fajr sunnah is closest to wajib but remains sunnah.

The daily prayers are accompanied by regular sunnah prayers called sunnan rawatib. This passage from Sharah al-Ashbah wa al-Nazair enumerates them and highlights that while all are emphasized, the Fajr sunnah holds a special status. Understanding this list and the nuanced debate about its obligation is essential for a mufti issuing fatwas on prayer practices.

Guided Path
1
Identify the complete list of sunnan rawatib
Memorize or recall the twelve rak'ahs distributed across the five daily prayers: 2 before Fajr, 4 before Zuhr, 2 after Zuhr, 2 after Maghrib, 2 after 'Isha.
Note: The text also mentions additional prayers like Tarawih and Witr, but these are not part of the sunnan rawatib.
2
Distinguish between sunnah mu'akkada and other categories
Understand that sunnah mu'akkada is a distinct level between wajib and ghayr mu'akkada. These are acts the Prophet consistently performed and rarely left.
In Hanafi usul, sunnah mu'akkada has a binding force but is not obligatory.
3
Analyze the special emphasis of Fajr sunnah
Note that the Fajr sunnah is especially emphasized because of the strong encouragement and deterrence associated with it. Some scholars, based on this emphasis, considered it wajib.
The text says it is 'close to wajib' (قریب واجبات کے).
4
Understand the intra-Hanafi ikhtilaf and the mufta bih
Recognize that there is a difference of opinion within the Hanafi school: some jurists held it wajib, but the relied-upon (mufta bih) position is that it remains sunnah mu'akkada.
The author explicitly states that the wajib opinion is 'غير مفتی‌بہ' (not relied upon).
5
Apply this knowledge in fatwa context
When asked about the Fajr sunnah, a mufti should state that it is sunnah mu'akkada and highly recommended, but not obligatory. Missing it is not sinful, but it is a great loss.
This aligns with the Hanafi fatwa hierarchy: the mufta bih takes precedence over less authoritative views.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
ترجمه: سنن مؤکده شب و روز میں بار‌ہ رکعتیں ہیں: دو رکعت فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعتیں ظہر سے پہلے اور دو رکعت ظہر کے بعد اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد۔ اور جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ سے پہلے اور چار رکعت جمعہ کے بعد۔ اور تراویح بیس رکعات ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ عشاء کے بعد رمضان کی راتوں میں۔ اور وتر کی نماز صاحبین کے قول پر۔ اور عیدین کی نماز دو روایوں میں سے ایک میں۔ اور صحیح قول کے مطابق کسوف کی نماز اور کہا گیا واجب ہے۔ اور نماز خوف اور استسقاء ایک قول پر۔
تشریح: اس بحث کی تکمیل پر مزید چند چیزیں بیان کی جارہی ہیں ان میں سے سنن مؤکدہ کی تفصیل ہے۔ سنن رواتب وہ سنتیں کہلاتی ہیں جو کہ مؤکدہ ہیں اسی وجہ سے انہیں سنن مؤکدہ بھی کہدیا جاتا ہے۔ سنن رواتب بارہ ہیں: دو رکعت نماز فجر سے پہلے اور چار رکعت ظہر سے پہلے، دو رکعت ظہر کے بعد، اور دو رکعت مغرب کے بعد، اور دو رکعت عشاء کے بعد۔ لیکن ان میں سے فجر سے پہلے والی دو رکعت تاکید و ترغیب و ترہیب کی وجہ سے قریب واجبات کے ہیں، اسی وجہ سے بعض فقہاء فجر کی سنتوں کے وجوب کے قائل ہیں اگرچہ یہ وجوب کا قول غیر مفتی‌بہ ہے۔
(بدائع الصنائع ج ١ ص: ٦٣٦)
Translation: The emphasized sunnahs of the night and day are twelve rak'ahs: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zuhr, two rak'ahs after Zuhr, two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after 'Isha. And in Friday prayer, four rak'ahs before Jumu'ah and four rak'ahs after. And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs with ten salams after 'Isha in the nights of Ramadan. And Witr prayer according to the two companions (Sahibayn). And the two 'Eid prayers according to one of the two narrations. And according to the correct statement, the eclipse prayer (kusuf) and it is said obligatory. And the prayer of fear (khawf) and the prayer for rain (istisqa) according to one statement.
Explanation: To complete this discussion, a few more things are being stated. Among them is the detail of the emphasized sunnahs. The sunnan rawatib are the sunnahs that are emphasized; for that reason they are also called sunnan mu'akkada. The sunnan rawatib are twelve: two rak'ahs before Fajr, four rak'ahs before Zuhr, two rak'ahs after Zuhr, two rak'ahs after Maghrib, and two rak'ahs after 'Isha. But among them, the two rak'ahs before Fajr are close to obligatory due to emphasis, encouragement, and deterrence; therefore some jurists hold the obligation of the Fajr sunnah, although this statement of obligation is not the relied-upon (mufta bih) opinion.
Source pages p. 167

Commentary
This passage lists the twelve sunnan rawatib (emphasized sunnah prayers) that are part of the daily prayers. The author first gives a summary translation, then an explanation. The key point is that while all twelve are sunnah mu'akkada, the Fajr sunnah is particularly emphasized, to the extent that some Hanafi scholars considered it obligatory (wajib). However, the relied-upon position (mufta bih) is that it remains sunnah, not wajib. The citation from Badai' al-Sanai' (vol. 1, p. 636) supports this.

Key Terms
سنن مؤکدہ (sunan mu'akkada): Emphasized sunnahs that the Prophet consistently performed and rarely left.
سنن رواتب (sunan rawatib): The regular sunnah prayers associated with the five daily prayers.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, the Fajr sunnah prayer is:
A) Wajib, and must be made up if missed.
B) Sunnah mu'akkada, and the mufta bih is that it is not wajib.
C) Sunnah ghayr mu'akkada, with no special emphasis.
D) Fard, as it is part of the obligatory prayer.

Key Takeaway
The twelve sunnan rawatib are sunnah mu'akkada; the Fajr sunnah is highly emphasized but remains sunnah, not wajib, in the relied-upon Hanafi position.

The Sunnah Prayers of Jumu'ah and Exiting Khilaf
Ruling on sunnah prayers of Jumu'ah with an intra-madhhab dispute.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi rule on Jumu'ah sunnah prayers and apply the principle of exiting khilaf in a fatwa context.

Core Idea
The Hanafi school rules four rak'ahs after Jumu'ah, but to exit the khilaf one may add two, following a key iftaa principle.

This lesson clarifies the sunnah prayers attached to Jumu'ah, which are an emphasized sunnah. You will learn the standard Hanafi position, a valid difference from Imam Abu Yusuf, and how the later school recommends a practice that accommodates both views—a vital skill for issuing fatwa.

Guided Path
1
Identify the rule
State the number of sunnah rak'ahs before and after Jumu'ah according to the Hanafi school as given in the passage.
The passage says four before and four after are sunnah mu'akkada.
2
Recognize the intra-madhhab difference
Note that Imam Abu Yusuf (part of Sahibayn) holds that the after-prayer is six rak'ahs, based on a narration from 'Ali.
This is a legitimate ikhtilaf within the school.
3
Understand the tarjih and exiting khilaf
The preferred (afdal) practice is to pray four then two, making six, to exit the difference while remaining within the valid range.
This exemplifies the iftaa principle of preferring a action that satisfies multiple valid opinions.
4
Apply the rule in fatwa
When asked, a mufti can state the relied-upon position (four) but should also mention the recommended practice to avoid khilaf.
The fatwa hierarchy: the mufta bihi is four, but the afdal is to add two.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وفي صلاة الجمعة: جمعہ کی نماز میں چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز سے پہلے سنت مؤکدہ ہیں اور چار رکعت جمعہ کی نماز کے بعد۔ اور امام ابو یوسف کے نزدیک مزید دو رکعت اور ہیں چار رکعت کے بعد، جیسا کہ طحطاوی علی مراقی الفلاح میں تصریح ہے: عند ابي يوسف السنة بعد الجمعة ست ركعات و هو مروى عن على والافضل ان يصلى اربعا ثم ركعتين للخروج من الخلاف۔
And in the Friday prayer: In the Friday prayer, four rak'ahs before the Friday prayer are emphasized sunnah, and four rak'ahs after the Friday prayer. And according to Imam Abu Yusuf, there are an additional two rak'ahs after the four, as stated in al-Tahtawi 'ala Maraqi al-Falah: 'According to Abu Yusuf, the sunnah after Jumu'ah is six rak'ahs, and it is narrated from 'Ali. And the preferred is that one prays four then two to exit the difference.'
Source pages p. 167

Commentary
This passage explains the sunnah prayers associated with Jumu'ah. The relied-upon Hanafi position is four rak'ahs before and four after. However, Imam Abu Yusuf narrated that the Prophet's practice was six after Jumu'ah, and this is supported by a narration from 'Ali (may Allah be pleased with him). To avoid the khilaf (disagreement), the preferred (afdal) is to pray four then an additional two, making six in total. This is a good example of the Hanafi principle of preferring a practice that accommodates valid differences.

Key Terms
سنت مؤکدہ (sunnah mu'akkada): Emphasized sunnah prayer.
صاحبین (Sahibayn): In this context, Imam Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani.
الخروج من الخلاف (al-khuruj min al-khilaf): Exiting a difference of opinion.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint

A) Two
B) Four
C) Six
D) None

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school holds four sunnah rak'ahs after Jumu'ah, but to honor a valid difference, it is afdal to pray four then two additional rak'ahs.

Tarawih Prayer: Twenty Rak'ahs, Timing, and Qada' Rulings
Ruling on Tarawih with expansion on number, time, and qada'

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on Tarawih's rak'ahs, time, and qada', and identify the mufta bihi position in the intra-Hanafi dispute.

Core Idea
Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs, sunnah mu'akkada, with no qada' after its time.

Tarawih is a beloved nightly prayer in Ramadan, but its exact ruling and make-up can be nuanced. This lesson unpacks the established Hanafi position: twenty rak'ahs, its proper time, and when—if ever—it can be made up. You will learn not only the rule but also the weight of different scholarly opinions within the school.

Guided Path
1
Identify the Rule and Its Authority
Read the passage to extract the key ruling: Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs, prayed in ten salams. Note the authority cited (majority of scholars, Badai' al-Sanai').
Remember: twenty rak'ahs is the relied-upon number in the Hanafi school.
2
Understand the Number and Manner
The text explains the structure: twenty rak'ahs in ten salams (two rak'ahs per salam), with a tarwiha (rest) after every two salams. Even praying four rak'ahs with a tashahhud is acceptable.
3
Determine the Time for Tarawih
Identify the time: after 'Isha and before Witr is preferred, but the entire night is valid. Some scholars restrict it to before Witr; the majority allow after 'Isha regardless of Witr.
The preferred time is after 'Isha and before Witr.
4
Analyze the Qada' Dispute and the Mufta Bihi
The passage presents three views on making up missed Tarawih: no qada', qada' within Ramadan until the next night, and qada' until Ramadan ends. Determine which is the operative position for fatwa.
The relied-upon view is that qada' is not required after the time has passed, as Tarawih is sunnah mu'akkada and sunnan are generally not made up.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
والتراويح عشرون ركعة: تراویح کی رکعات بیس ہیں دس سلاموں کے ساتھ، یہی جمہور علماء کا قول ہے۔ اگر کسی نے چار چار رکعت پڑھی اور قعدہ اولیٰ کیا تو یہ بھی درست ہے۔ و اما قدرها فعشرون ركعة في عشر تسليمات في خمس ترویحات كل تسلمتين ترويحة وهذا قول عامة العلماء (بدائع الصنائع، ج ١ ص: ٦٤٤) بعد العشاء: بعض فقہاء کہتے ہیں کہ تراویح کا وقت عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے ہے۔ بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ پوری رات تراویح کا وقت ہے۔ جمہور علماء کی رائے یہ ہے کہ عشاء کے بعد تراویح کے وقت شروع ہو جاتا ہے خواہ وتر سے پہلے پڑھ لیں یا بعد میں اگرچہ افضل عشاء کے بعد اور وتر سے پہلے پڑھنا ہے۔ تراویح کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے، ظہیر یہ وغیرہ میں اس کی صراحت ہے۔ اسی وجہ سے کہا گیا کہ اگر تراویح چھوٹ جائیں تو وقت نکل جانے کے بعد ان کی قضا نہیں ہے۔ بعض علماء فرماتے ہیں کہ جب تک رمضان نہ گذرے تو قضا پڑھی جائے گی، اور بعض کی رائے یہ ہے کہ جب تک دوسری رات نہ آجائے اس وقت تک قضا تراویح پڑھی جاسکتی ہیں۔
And Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs: The rak'ahs of Tarawih are twenty with ten salams; this is the statement of the majority of scholars. If someone prays four rak'ahs with a first tashahhud (qa'dah ula), that is also correct. And as for its number, it is twenty rak'ahs in ten taslims in five tarwihas (rests): every two taslims constitute a tarwiha. This is the statement of the general scholars (Badai' al-Sanai', vol. 1, p. 644). After 'Isha: Some jurists say that the time of Tarawih is after 'Isha and before Witr. Some opine that the entire night is the time for Tarawih. The majority of scholars are of the opinion that the time for Tarawih begins after 'Isha, whether one prays it before Witr or after, although the preferred is to pray after 'Isha and before Witr. Tarawih prayer is an emphasized sunnah (sunnah mu'akkada); this is explicitly stated in al-Zuhayrah and others. For this reason, it has been said that if Tarawih is missed, there is no qada' after the time has passed. Some scholars say that qada' can be performed as long as Ramadan has not passed, and some opine that qada' can be performed until the next night comes.
Source pages p. 167

Commentary
This passage details the ruling and manner of Tarawih prayer. The number of rak'ahs is twenty, prayed in sets of two rak'ahs with a salam after each, totaling ten salams. The preferred time is after 'Isha and before Witr, but it can be prayed any time during the night. Tarawih is a sunnah mu'akkada, but unlike other sunan, it is not made up (qada') after its time has elapsed; however, there is some difference among scholars regarding qada' within Ramadan.

Key Terms
تراویح (tarawih): Twenty rak'ahs of sunnah prayer performed in Ramadan after 'Isha.
قضا (qada'): Making up a missed prayer after its prescribed time.
سنة مؤكدة (sunnah mu'akkada): An emphasized sunnah, routinely performed by the Prophet; omission is disliked but not sinful like wajib.

Key Terms from Source Passage

B) It is permissible to make them up at any time.
C) It is not required; there is no qada' after the time.
D) Only if one intends qada' before the next Tarawih.

Key Takeaway
Tarawih is twenty rak'ahs, sunnah mu'akkada, prayed after 'Isha; missed prayers are not made up after the time.

The Legal Status of Witr Prayer: Wajib in the Hanafi School
Discusses ikhtilaf on Witr's legal status.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the three narrations from Abu Hanifa on Witr and identify the mufta bih position (wajib) with its evidence.

Core Idea
Witr is wajib in the Hanafi school, not merely sunnah—the fatwa is on obligation to safeguard its practice.

The status of Witr prayer is a classic case of intra-madhhab ikhtilaf. Imam Abu Hanifa has three reported views, and the well-known position adopted for fatwa is that it is wajib. This lesson dissects the narrations, the reasoning of the Sahibayn and Imam al-Shafi'i, and why the Hanafi school ultimately settled on obligation.

Guided Path
1
Identify the three narrations from Abu Hanifa
List the three reported views: sunnah mu'akkada, wajib, and fard. Note which narrations are attributed to which chain.
The fard narration via Hammad ibn Zayd is weak and not relied upon.
2
Understand the stance of the Sahibayn
Abu Yusuf and Muhammad adopted the sunnah narration, yet they did not permit praying Witr sitting without an excuse. Analyze why: because the Prophet never did so and to preserve the emphasis.
This shows even those who held sunnah treated it with high regard.
3
Recognise the mashhur and mufta bih
The well-known (mashhur) statement is that Witr is wajib, and upon this is the fatwa. Identify the authoritative basis for this preference.
Later Hanafi masters (e.g., al-Haskafi) confirmed wajib as the relied-upon position.
4
Note the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical consequence: ruling on praying while sitting, congregation in Ramadan, and the sin of leaving Witr.
Those holding sunnah allow sitting without excuse; those holding wajib require standing unless valid excuse.
5
Apply the fatwa hierarchy
Use the hierarchy: zahir al-riwayah > nawadir > fatawa mutakhkhirin. The wajib position is from the later authoritative fatwa works.
Thus the mufti must give fatwa on wajib, even if other opinions exist.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
صلاة الوتر: صاحبین کے نزدیک نماز وتر سنت ہے، حضرت امام صاحب کے نزدیک وتر کے بارے میں تین روایات ہیں جن میں سے ایک یہ ہے کہ وتر کی نماز سنت مؤکدہ ہے، صاحبین نے اسی روایت کو لے کر وتر کی سنیت کی بات کہی ہے اور مشہور قول وجوب کا ہے اس پر فتویٰ ہے۔ عنه انه سنة و به اخذ ابويوسف و محمد و الشافعي رحمهم الله وقالوا انه سنة مؤكدة أكد من سائر السنن المؤقته (بدائع زكريا، ص: ۲۰۶) تیسری روایت بواسطه حماد بن زید نماز وتر کے فرض کی ہے۔ نماز وتر کے سلسلہ میں ایک قول وجوب کا بھی ہے اس لئے صاحبین بھی بدون عذر بیٹھ کر نماز وتر کی اجازت نہیں دیتے یا اس لئے کہ آپ صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم نے نماز وتر بیٹھ کر نہیں پڑھی، جن فقہاء نے نماز وتر کی سنیت کی بناء پر ان کو بدون عذر بیٹھ کر پڑھنے کی اجازت دی ہے وہ کسی پر ہیں نیز رمضان میں وتر جماعت کے ساتھ پڑھنا اصلی ہے اپنے گھر میں تنہا پڑھنے سے جیسا کہ ظہیر بیا اور خانیہ میں مذکور ہے۔
Witr prayer: According to the Sahibayn (Abu Yusuf and Muhammad), Witr prayer is sunnah. According to Imam Abu Hanifa, there are three narrations regarding Witr, one of which is that Witr prayer is an emphasized sunnah (sunnah mu'akkada). The Sahibayn took this narration and stated the sunnah nature of Witr. And the well-known (mashhur) statement is that it is obligatory (wajib), and upon this is the fatwa. It is narrated from him (Abu Hanifa) that it is sunnah, and Abu Yusuf, Muhammad, and al-Shafi'i (may Allah have mercy on them) adopted this, and they said it is an emphasized sunnah, more emphasized than other time-bound sunnahs (Badai' Zakarai, p. 206). The third narration through Hammad ibn Zayd is that Witr prayer is obligatory (fard). Regarding Witr prayer, there is also a statement of obligation (wujub); therefore the Sahibayn do not permit praying Witr while sitting without an excuse, or because the Prophet (peace be upon him) never prayed Witr sitting. Those jurists who, based on the sunnah nature of Witr, permit praying it sitting without an excuse, are few. Also, in Ramadan, praying Witr with congregation is primary, compared to praying alone at home, as mentioned in al-Zuhayra and al-Khaniyya.
Source pages p. 167

Commentary
This passage addresses the legal status of Witr prayer, a topic of notable ikhtilaf within the Hanafi school. Imam Abu Hanifa has three narrations: that Witr is sunnah mu'akkada (the narration adopted by Sahibayn and Imam al-Shafi'i), that it is wajib (the mashhur and the basis of fatwa), and that it is fard (a weak narration via Hammad ibn Zayd). The relied-upon position for fatwa is that Witr is wajib. Consequently, the Sahibayn, even though they considered it sunnah, still did not permit praying Witr sitting without an excuse, as the Prophet never did so. This shows that even within the range of valid ikhtilaf, the ruling carries significant weight. Additionally, Witr with congregation in Ramadan is preferred over individual prayer.

Key Terms
وتر (witr): The odd-numbered prayer performed after the night prayers, usually 1, 3, 5, 7, 9, or 11 rak'ahs.
مشہور قول (mashhur qawl): The well-known and dominant opinion within the school.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the relied-upon (mufta bih) position regarding Witr prayer in the Hanafi school?
A) Sunnah mu'akkada
B) Wajib
C) Fard
D) Mustahabb

Key Takeaway
In the Hanafi school, Witr is wajib (mufta bih); the fatwa is based on obligation to ensure it is not neglected.

Eid Prayer: Wajib by Mufta Bih
States the Hanafi ruling on Eid prayer as wajib, with a qawl that it is sunnah.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the mufta bih ruling for Eid prayer in the Hanafi school, state the tarjih mechanism that elevates it over a conflicting qawl, and apply this principle to other similar cases.

Core Idea
The mufta bih on Eid prayer is wajib, overriding earlier sunnah classification.

In the Hanafi school, the ruling on Eid prayer is a neat case study of how later tarjih (preference) can settle a seemingly ambiguous textual history. While an early authoritative text like al-Jami' al-Saghir of Imam Muhammad called it sunnah, the relied-upon position for fatwa is that it is wajib. This lesson unpacks that shift and equips you to handle similar instances where early and later authorities appear to diverge.

Guided Path
1
Identify the issue
What is the legal nature (hukm) of the two Eid prayers according to the Hanafi school? There are two quoted opinions: sunnah and wajib.
Sunnah here means sunnah mu'akkada (emphasized sunnah).
2
Locate the conflicting qawls
The earlier qawl, found in al-Jami' al-Saghir, calls it sunnah. The later mufta bih qawl calls it wajib. Identify which qawl is cited as the correct one.
Text explicitly says 'wa al-sahih annaha wajiba'.
3
Apply the tarjih mechanism
Understand why the later qawl becomes the mufta bih. Tarjih is based on later ijtihad by the majority of Hanafi scholars (asbābunā), not merely on textual age.
Tarjih often involves examining strength of evidence, practice of the ummah, and consistency with other rulings.
4
Formulate the fatwa principle
The mufta bih is the operative position for issuing fatwas. Even if earlier texts say otherwise, the mufti follows the later consensus of the school.
This illustrates the principle 'al-mufta bih huwa al-mu'tamad'.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وصلاة العيدين: مذہب حنفی میں مفتی‌بہ قول تو یہی ہے کہ عیدین کی نماز واجب ہے لیکن ایک قول سنت کا بھی ہے، وسماه سنة في الجامع الصغير انها واجبة بالسنة ام هي سنة مؤكدة الى قوله والصحيح انها واجبة وهذا قول اصحابنا ۔ (بدائع زکریا ج ا س: ۶۱۶)
And the two 'Eid prayers: In the Hanafi school, the mufta bih statement is that the two 'Eid prayers are wajib, but there is also a statement that they are sunnah. He (the author of al-Jami' al-Saghir) called it sunnah, (but then said) that it is wajib by sunnah, or is it an emphasized sunnah, up to his saying: 'And the correct is that it is wajib, and this is the statement of our companions.' (Badai' Zakarai, vol. 1, p. 616)
Source pages p. 167

Commentary
This passage clarifies the Hanafi position on 'Eid prayer. The mufta bih (relied-upon for fatwa) opinion is that it is wajib. Although some early texts, like al-Jami' al-Saghir, referred to it as sunnah, the correct position in the school is that it is wajib. This is the statement of the majority of Hanafi scholars. The passage illustrates how earlier formulations may be overridden by later ijtihad and the consolidation of the madhhab.

Key Terms
عیدین (idayn): The two 'Eids: 'Eid al-Fitr and 'Eid al-Adha.
مفتی‌بہ (mufta bih): The opinion that is relied upon for issuing fatwas.
جامع الصغیر (al-Jami' al-Saghir): A foundational Hanafi text by Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani, part of Zahir al-Riwayah.

Key Takeaway
